\[
F(t,P)=A\,P\,e^{-kt}+A\,\frac{P^2}{B P+1}
\]
with \(A=0.3156057016002752\), \(k=0.05405074842498068\), \(B=9.870854086995406\).

Key structural facts about GT:

- It is a sum of **(i)** a separable term \( (\text{const})\cdot P\cdot e^{-k t}\) and **(ii)** a **purely \(P\)-rational** term \(A P^2/(BP+1)\) independent of \(t\).
- For fixed \(P\neq 0\), the \(t\)-dependence is exactly a single exponential \(e^{-kt}\) plus a constant offset (in \(t\)).
- No sines/cosines, no logs, no \(\max\), no \(|P|\), no \(t^2\), no \(1/(t+\cdot)\), etc., can remain unless their coefficients are set to 0.
- The \(P\)-dependence includes a rational function with denominator linear in \(P\). Any candidate lacking a \(1/(aP+b)\)-type structure (or an algebraically equivalent one) cannot reproduce \(A P^2/(BP+1)\) for all \(P\).

Now check each candidate for whether its form can be parameter-set to exactly \(F(t,P)\).

---

### 1
\(P c0 +\) sine terms \(+\) linear \(t\) \(+\) constant \(+\log(Pc7+1)\sin(\cdot)\).
- Can zero out sine/log/linear/constant terms, leaving only \(P c0\), but GT needs \(P e^{-kt}\) and a rational \(P^2/(BP+1)\).
- No way to create \(e^{-kt}\) or the rational term. **No match.**

### 2
Same as (1) but with \(\log(c7|P|+1)\).
- Same issue; also \(|P|\) incompatible unless coefficient 0. Still cannot form GT. **No match.**

### 3
\(P c0 + P^{c1} c2 + \sin(\cdot)+ c6 t + c7 e^{c8 t}\).
- Can set sine and linear terms to 0. Remaining: \(P c0 + c2 P^{c1} + c7 e^{c8 t}\).
- GT needs \(P e^{-kt}\) (product of \(P\) and exponential), but here exponential term is independent of \(P\). No product \(P e^{\cdot t}\) term. **No match.**

### 4
\(P^2 c0 e^{c1 t} + P c2 + P^{c3} c4 e^{c5 t} + c6 e^{c7/(c8+t)} + c9\).
- Has \(P^2 e^{(\cdot)t}\) and \(P^{c3} e^{(\cdot)t}\) but GT needs \(P e^{-kt}\) plus a **\(t\)-independent** rational in \(P\).
- No rational \(P^2/(BP+1)\) possible; only polynomials times exponentials. **No match.**

### 5
\(P c0 + \frac{P c1}{P+c2} + \sin(\cdot)+ c6 t + c7 + c8 e^{c9 t}\).
- The rational piece is \(\frac{P c1}{P+c2}\), which is degree 1 over degree 1; GT rational is \(\frac{A P^2}{BP+1}\) (degree 2 over degree 1).
- You cannot make \(\frac{P c1}{P+c2}\) equal \(\frac{A P^2}{BP+1}\) for all \(P\) (growth differs: left \(\sim c1\) as \(P\to\infty\), right \(\sim (A/B)P\)).
- Also lacks \(P e^{-kt}\) unless using \(c8 e^{c9 t}\), but that term is not multiplied by \(P\). **No match.**

### 6
\(P c0 + P^{c1} c2 \log(c3 t+1)+\sin(\cdot)+c7 t\).
- Any \(\log(c3 t+1)\) dependence cannot equal \(e^{-kt}\) for all \(t\).
- No rational \(P^2/(BP+1)\). **No match.**

### 7
\(P^{c0} c1 e^{c2 t} + c3\tanh(\cdot)+ c6 e^{c7\sin(\cdot)}\).
- Can zero tanh and last term, leaving \(c1 P^{c0} e^{c2 t}\). This can match the **first** GT term by setting \(c0=1\), \(c2=-k\), \(c1=A\).
- But then there is no way to add the required \(A P^2/(BP+1)\) term (no rational-in-\(P\) additive component). **No match.**

### 8
\(P^{c0} c1 e^{c2 t} + P^{c3} c4 e^{c5 t} + c6 t e^{c7 t}\).
- Can kill the last term. Remaining is sum of two separable power*exponential terms.
- Second GT term is \(t\)-independent rational in \(P\), not representable as \(P^{c3} e^{c5 t}\) unless \(c5=0\) (making it \(P^{c3}c4\)), but a pure power \(P^{c3}\) cannot equal \(P^2/(BP+1)\) for all \(P\). **No match.**

### 9
Linear in \(P\) plus sines including \(\sin(\log(|P|))\).
- Must zero sines to avoid oscillatory dependence; then only linear in \(P\) and \(t\) remains, cannot match GT. **No match.**

### 10
Contains \(P^{1/5}/\sqrt t\), linear \(P\), polynomial in \(t\), and \(e^{\sin}\).
- Must zero non-GT structures; left with linear \(P\) only, cannot match. **No match.**

### 11
\(P c0 + P^{c1} c2 + P^{c3} c4 + \sin(\cdot)+ c8 t\).
- After zeroing sine and \(t\), it’s a sum of powers of \(P\) only; cannot produce \(P e^{-kt}\) (needs \(t\)) nor rational \(P^2/(BP+1)\). **No match.**

### 12
\(P c0 + \sin(\cdot)+ c4 t + c5 + c6 e^{c7 t}\).
- No \(P e^{c7 t}\) product; exponential term independent of \(P\). No rational term. **No match.**

### 13
\(c0 e^{c1/(c2+t)} + c3\max(0,P+c4) + c5\log(c6 e^{c7\sin(\cdot)}+1)\).
- Piecewise max and \(1/(t+\cdot)\) exponential cannot match GT’s smooth \(e^{-kt}\) and rational term. **No match.**

### 14
\(P c0 + P^{c1} c2 e^{c3 t}\log(c4 t+1) + c5 e^{c6/(c7+t)} + c8\).
- Has \(\log(c4 t+1)\) and \(e^{c6/(c7+t)}\) which cannot be made into \(e^{-kt}\) for all \(t\) except by zeroing them, leaving only \(P c0 + c8\), insufficient. **No match.**

### 15
Includes \(P c0|P|^{c1}\), \(P c2\), \(P c3 t^{c4}\log(|P|)\), \(t e^{t}\), etc.
- To match GT must remove \(|P|\), logs, powers of \(t\), etc., leaving at best polynomial in \(P\), not the needed rational and \(P e^{-kt}\). **No match.**

### 16
Linear \(P\) terms + sine + linear \(t\) + \(\max(0,P+c8)\).
- Must zero sine/max/linear \(t\) to avoid non-GT behavior; left linear in \(P\) only. **No match.**

### 17
\(c0 t e^{c1 t} + c2 |P|^{1/3}/t^5 + c3\log(\cdot)\log(\cdot)\).
- Singular at \(t=0\) and \(|P|^{1/3}\) etc.; cannot equal GT for all \(t,P\). **No match.**

### 18
A complicated expression with common denominator \(c2+c3 e^{c4 t}\), mixing \(P\) and \(t\) in rational-in-\(e^{c4 t}\) way.
- GT’s \(t\)-dependence is \(P e^{-kt}\) plus \(t\)-independent term. Any term like \(P \cdot \frac{t^{c1}}{c2+c3 e^{c4 t}}\) cannot equal \(P e^{-kt}\) for all \(t\) unless it reduces exactly to an exponential; but \(\frac{1}{a+b e^{c4 t}}\) is not a pure exponential for all \(t\).
- Also no way to create \(P^2/(BP+1)\) (depends on \(P\) rationally, not on \(e^{t}\)). **No match.**

### 19
\(P c0 + P^{c1} c2 \sin(\cdot)+ \sin(\cdot)+ c8 t\).
- Must zero sine terms; left linear in \(P\) and \(t\). **No match.**

### 20
\(P c0 + P c1 \log(c2/(P+c3)+1)+ \sin(\cdot)+ c7 t + c8\).
- Log in \(P\) cannot become \(P^2/(BP+1)\) for all \(P\). Also lacks \(P e^{-kt}\). **No match.**

### 21
Same as (20) with \(|P|\). **No match.**

### 22
\(P c0 + P^{c1} c2 \cos(\cdot)+ c5 t + c6\).
- Must zero cosine and \(t\) to avoid oscillation/linear; left linear in \(P\). **No match.**

### 23
\(P c0 + \sin(\cdot)+ c4 + c5 t + c6 e^{c7\sin(\cdot)}\).
- No rational term; no \(P e^{-kt}\) product. **No match.**

### 24
\(P c0 + P^{c1} c2 e^{c3 t} + c4 e^{c5/(c6+t)} + c7 + c8\max(0,P+c9)\).
- Can set max and \(e^{1/(t+\cdot)}\) to 0, leaving \(P c0 + c2 P^{c1} e^{c3 t} + c7\).
- Still no \(P^2/(BP+1)\) rational term. **No match.**

### 25
\(P^{c0} c1 e^{c2 t} + c3 e^{c4/(c5+t)} + c6 + c7\max(0,P+c8)\).
- Can match first term as in (7), but cannot generate the rational \(P\)-term. **No match.**

### 26
\(P c0 + P c1 e^{P c2} + P^{c3} c4 \log(c5 t+1)+ \sin(\cdot)+ c9 t\).
- Has \(e^{P c2}\) (wrong coupling) and \(\log(t)\). Cannot reduce to GT. **No match.**

### 27
Linear \(P\) + sine + linear \(t\) + power \((c8 t+1)^{c9}\).
- Cannot form \(P e^{-kt}\) and rational \(P^2/(BP+1)\). **No match.**

### 28
\(P^{c0} c1 t^{c2} + c3 t^2 + c4 t + c5 + c6 \sin(c7\log(Pc8+1)+c9)\).
- Must kill sine and polynomial terms; remaining \(P^{c0} t^{c2}\) cannot equal \(P e^{-kt}\). **No match.**

### 29
Same as (28) with \(|P|\). **No match.**

### 30
\(P c0 + P c1 e^{c2 t} + P^{c3} c4 + \sin(\cdot)+ c8 t + c9\).
- The term \(P c1 e^{c2 t}\) can match \(A P e^{-kt}\) by \(c1=A, c2=-k\).
- But the remaining needed term is \(A P^2/(BP+1)\), while candidate offers only \(P^{c3} c4\) (a pure power) plus optional constants/linear/sine which must be zero. A pure power cannot equal that rational function for all \(P\). **No match.**

### 31
\(P^{c0} c1 t^{c2} + \text{poly in }t + c6 \log(c7 e^{P^{c8} c9}+1)\).
- Wrong \(P\)-dependence (log of exp of power), no way to get rational \(P^2/(BP+1)\) and \(P e^{-kt}\). **No match.**

### 32
\(P c0 \log(1+c1/P) + c2\max(0,P+c3)+ c4 e^{c5/(c6+t)} + c7\cos(P^{c8}c9)\).
- Non-analytic at \(P=0\) due to \(\log(1+c1/P)\); GT is analytic in \(P\) near 0. Also max/cos terms incompatible unless zeroed, leaving log structure not equal to GT. **No match.**

### 33
\(P c0 e^{c1 e^{c2+c3 t}} + P^{c4} c5 e^{c6 t} + c7 t e^{c8 t}\).
- Double exponential in \(t\) cannot become \(e^{-kt}\) except by zeroing; then still no rational term. **No match.**

### 34
\(P^2 c0 e^{c1 t} + P c2 + P c3 + \sin(\cdot)+ c7 t + c8\).
- No rational \(P^2/(BP+1)\); only polynomial in \(P\). **No match.**

### 35
\(\frac{P c0}{c1+c2 e^{c3 t}} + \frac{P c4 e^{c3 t}}{c1+c2 e^{c3 t}} + \frac{c5 t}{c1+c2 e^{c3 t}} + c6 e^{c7 t}\log(P c8+1)\).
- The first two terms combine to \(P\frac{c0+c4 e^{c3 t}}{c1+c2 e^{c3 t}}\), which is a Möbius transform in \(e^{c3 t}\), not a pure exponential \(P e^{-kt}\) for all \(t\) unless it degenerates to a constant (by proportionality), but then it cannot produce \(e^{-kt}\).
- Log term in \(P\) cannot produce \(P^2/(BP+1)\). **No match.**

### 36
Same as (35) with \(|P|\). **No match.**

### 37
\(P c0 + c1 e^{c2/(c3+t)} + c4 + c5\log(c6 e^{c7 t}+1)\).
- No \(P e^{-kt}\) (only linear \(P\) plus other \(t\)-only terms). No rational in \(P\). **No match.**

### 38
Similar to (35) but with \(\log(c7 e^{c8 t}+1)\) (no \(P\) in log).
- Still cannot produce \(P e^{-kt}\) (Möbius in \(e^{t}\)), and no rational \(P^2/(BP+1)\). **No match.**

### 39
\(P c0 + \sin(\cdot)+ c4 t + c5 \log(Pc6+1)\log(c7 t+1)\).
- Product of logs cannot become \(P e^{-kt}\) or rational term. **No match.**

### 40
\(\frac{P^2 c0}{P^2 c1+1} + P^{c2} c3 \log(P c4+1) + c5 + c6 t^2 + c7 t + c8 e^{P c9}\).
- First term is rational in \(P\) but denominator is \(1+c1 P^2\), not \(1+BP\). No parameter choice makes \(1+c1 P^2\) equal \(1+BP\) for all \(P\).
- Other terms must be zeroed; still wrong rational structure. **No match.**

### 41
\(P c0 + P c1 + c2 e^{c3/(c4+t)} + c5 + c6\log(c7 e^{c8 t}+1)\).
- No \(P e^{-kt}\) product; no rational \(P^2/(BP+1)\). **No match.**

### 42
\(P c0 + \frac{P c1}{P^{c1}+c3} + c4 e^{c5/(c6+t)}\).
- The rational-like term uses \(P^{c1}\) in denominator; to make denominator linear in \(P\) would require \(c1=1\), giving \(\frac{P c1}{P+c3}\) which (as in candidate 5) cannot equal \(A P^2/(BP+1)\) for all \(P\) (wrong asymptotics).
- Also lacks \(P e^{-kt}\). **No match.**

### 43
\(P c0 + \frac{P c1}{P+c2} + \frac{P c3}{P+c4} + \sin(\cdot)+ c8 t + c9\).
- Sum of two degree-1/degree-1 terms cannot equal degree-2/degree-1 term \(P^2/(BP+1)\) for all \(P\) (again asymptotics: each fraction tends to constant; sum tends to constant; GT grows \(\sim (A/B)P\)).
- No \(P e^{-kt}\). **No match.**

### 44
\(\frac{P^2 c0}{P^2 c1+1} + P^{c2} c3 \log(P c4+1) + c5 t^2 + c6 t + c7 + c8 e^{c9 t}\).
- Same wrong rational denominator \(1+c1 P^2\). Also no \(P e^{-kt}\) product. **No match.**

### 45
\(P c0 + \frac{P c1}{P c2+1} + P^{c3} c4 + \sin(\cdot)+ c8 t + c9\).
- \(\frac{P c1}{1+c2 P}\) is degree-1/degree-1, not \(P^2/(1+BP)\).
- Even adding \(P^{c3}\) cannot create exactly \(P^2/(1+BP)\) for all \(P\). **No match.**

### 46
Same core issue as (40)/(44): \(\frac{P^2 c0}{P^2 c1+1}\) has quadratic denominator. **No match.**

### 47
\(P\cdot P^{c0} c1 + P c2 + P^{c3} c4 \log(P c5+1) + c6 t^2 + c7 t + c8\).
- No \(e^{-kt}\). Log term in \(P\) not allowed. **No match.**

### 48
\(P c0 + c1 e^{c2/(c3+t)} + c4 + c5\log(c6 e^{c7 t}+1) + c8 e^{c9 t}\).
- Exponentials are \(t\)-only, not multiplied by \(P\); no rational \(P^2/(BP+1)\). **No match.**

### 49
\(P c0 + \sin(\cdot)+ c4 t + c5 \sin(c6\log(c7|P|+1)+c8)\).
- Must zero sines and linear \(t\); left linear \(P\) only. **No match.**

### 50
\(P^{c0} c1 e^{c2 t} + c3 t^2 + c4 t + c5\).
- Can set polynomial terms to 0 and match \(A P e^{-kt}\) via \(c0=1,c1=A,c2=-k\).
- But cannot add the required rational \(A P^2/(BP+1)\). **No match.**

---

No candidate contains (or can be reduced to) a sum of **(i)** \(P e^{-kt}\) and **(ii)** a \(t\)-independent **linear-denominator rational** \(P^2/(BP+1)\). Several can match the first term alone (7, 25, 30, 50), and a few have rational-in-\(P\) pieces but of the wrong degree/denominator (5, 42, 43, 45, 40/44/46). None can match both parts simultaneously for all \(t,P\).

[NO MATCH]

Conclusion: No match

GT Equivalence Verification (BPG1)
============================================================
GT: c0*P*exp(-c1*t) + c2*P**c3/(c4*P + c5)
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the Ground Truth:

**GT: 0.3156*P*exp(-0.0541*t) + 0.3156*P²/(9.871*P + 1)**

The GT has two terms:
1. A term proportional to P*exp(-c₁*t) — exponential decay in t, linear in P
2. A rational function P²/(c₄*P + c₅) — no t dependence

Let me analyze each candidate systematically.

**Key structural requirements:**
- Must have P*exp(αt) type term (exponential in t)
- Must have P²/(aP+b) type rational term
- No other basis functions (sin, log, polynomial in t, etc.) unless their coefficients can be zeroed

Let me go through each candidate:

### Candidate 1: P*c0 + c1*sin(c2*t+c3) + c4*t + c5 + c6*log(P*c7+1)*sin(c8*t+c9)
No exp(-ct) term for P. Has sin and log*sin terms. Cannot produce P*exp(-ct). **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 2: Similar to 1 with Abs(P). Same issue. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 3: P*c0 + P^c1*c2 + c3*sin(c4*t+c5) + c6*t + c7*exp(c8*t)
Has exp(c8*t) but not multiplied by P. Has P^c1 but not P²/(aP+b). Cannot produce P*exp(-ct). **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 4: P²*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c2 + P^c3*c4*exp(c5*t) + c6*exp(c7/(c8+t)) + c9
- P²*c0*exp(c1*t): If c1=0, this gives P²*c0 (not the rational form needed)
- P^c3*c4*exp(c5*t): Could be P*exp(-0.054t) if c3=1
- c6*exp(c7/(c8+t)): Cannot become P²/(aP+1) 
- Need P²/(aP+1) which is a rational function, not available here. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 5: P*c0 + P*c1/(P+c2) + c3*sin(c4*t+c5) + c6*t + c7 + c8*exp(c9*t)
- P*c1/(P+c2) = c1*P/(P+c2). With common denominator: c1*P/(P+c2).
  Note: P²/(aP+b) = P*P/(aP+b) = (1/a)*P*(aP)/(aP+b) = (1/a)*P*(aP+b-b)/(aP+b) = (1/a)*P - (b/a)*P/(aP+b)
  So P²/(9.871P+1) = (1/9.871)*P - (1/9.871)*P/(9.871P+1)
  
  Rewriting GT: 0.3156*P*exp(-0.054t) + 0.3156*[P/9.871 - P/(9.871*(9.871P+1))]
  = 0.3156*P*exp(-0.054t) + 0.03197*P - 0.003238*P/(9.871P+1)

  Candidate 5: P*(c0) + P*c1/(P+c2) + c3*sin(c4*t+c5) + c6*t + c7 + c8*exp(c9*t)
  
  Set c3=0 (kill sin), c6=0 (kill t), c7=0, then:
  P*c0 + P*c1/(P+c2) + c8*exp(c9*t)
  
  But we need P*exp(-0.054t), not just exp(c9*t). The exp term isn't multiplied by P. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 6-29: Let me scan for candidates with both P*exp(ct) and P²/(P+c) structure...

### Candidate 30: P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P^c3*c4 + c5*sin(c6*t+c7) + c8*t + c9
- P*c1*exp(c2*t): ✓ can give P*exp(-0.054t)
- P^c3*c4: This is just P^c3, not P²/(aP+b). Cannot produce rational function. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 34: P²*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c2 + P*c3 + c4*sin(c5*t+c6) + c7*t + c8
- P²*c0*exp(c1*t): If c1≠0, this has t-dependence on P² term, but GT's rational term has no t-dependence. If c1=0, gives P²*c0 (not rational). Need P*exp(-ct) but only have P*c2. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 45: P*c0 + P*c1/(P*c2+1) + P^c3*c4 + c5*sin(c6*t+c7) + c8*t + c9
- P*c1/(P*c2+1): This gives a rational term. P²/(aP+b) can be decomposed as shown above.
- But no P*exp(ct) term. **NO MATCH**

### Candidate 50: P^c0*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3*t² + c4*t + c5
- P^c0*c1*exp(c2*t): Only one such term. Need two different functional forms. **NO MATCH**

After careful analysis, **none** of the candidates can exactly reproduce the GT.
